msg:I recently stayed at the Oriental Hotel, which is known for its grand size and prestigious five-star rating. However, my experience was far from what one would expect from such a highly rated establishment.

Firstly, the hotel feels outdated. The furniture in the room was old and worn, which gave the space a tired and neglected atmosphere. Additionally, the cleanliness was not up to standard, which is a basic expectation for any hotel, especially a five-star one.

Service was another significant letdown. On one occasion, I requested an iron to press my clothes. I called the front desk multiple times‚Äîmore than four, to be exact‚Äîand even reached out to the duty manager. Despite my repeated requests, it took over an hour for the iron to arrive. When I finally encountered the staff member delivering it, she was smiling, seemingly oblivious to the inconvenience caused by the delay.

Other aspects of the stay were equally disappointing. The mini bar in my room was empty, and the shower had issues, with water spraying from the handle, making it difficult to use properly. On the positive side, the breakfast was enjoyable, providing a nice start to the day amidst an otherwise frustrating experience.

In conclusion, despite its impressive size and five-star rating, the Oriental Hotel fell short in many critical areas. The outdated furniture, cleanliness issues, poor service, and malfunctioning amenities all contributed to a very disappointing stay. I would not recommend this hotel based on my experience.

Take the subway 2 stops to Beijing bu xing jie, plenty of shops and vibrant place, it‚Äôs a must go. Yuexiu Park metro station is 5 min walk, and next door is a Starbucks and McDonalds.  Across the street is a new mall with lots of Chinese restaurants. It‚Äôs also about a 10 minute walk from Guangzhou‚Äôs famous clothing wholesale markets.  

Hotel lobby is huge and totally fabulous! Staying here makes you feel like you are living a life of luxury, but still at a reasonable price.   One thing I would tell the staff to improve :  showers need to be scrubbed better because any mold in the shower is unacceptable, even a little.  This is a common problem in China, different standards than western cultures I guess. Otherwise, this is the place to stay.  Standard Rooms here are a lot larger than at the China Hotel next door, and usually rooms rates for both properties are similar.  Why not stay at Dong Fang and get a nicer room for the same price ?

The Oriental Hotel, a garden-style hotel, has pavilions and waterside pavilions on the first floor, where you can take a stroll. The hall is magnificent. During the Spring Festival, the hall is decorated with joy and many guests are still taking pictures here. The elite room in Building 1 is more spacious, the room decoration is good, the facilities are high-grade, and the bedding is more comfortable. The room has good lighting, and the bathroom is dry and wet (slightly regrettable is that the window of the room faces a road. At night, there is noise from various vehicles passing by, but I can accept the noise. It should be that I am in a good mood, because the front desk of the hotel two A girl upgraded my room for free on the second day of my stay üòÑ). The hotel is about 500m away from Yuexiu Park Station of Metro Line 2, and it is fast and convenient to go there. Opposite the hotel is Liuhua Lake Park. It is very cool to run here. Running around the lake is about 2.5 miles. I ran more than 2 laps, which is a quarter of the distance of the marathon. In the park, green trees cover the blooming flowers, and various water birds perch and fly along the lake. There are also bonsai exhibitions in the park. There is a "South China Sea Fishing Village" that has a good environment and delicious dishes, and it is also a good place to drink morning tea. The hotel staff are patient and enthusiastic, especially the girls at the front desk. Among them, a girl surnamed Liu and one of her colleagues wanted to make up the difference in the afternoon of February 4, 2022 and change to a higher quality room. Promised to give me a free upgrade to the elite room in Building 1 on the same day, thank them very much. I wish them a smooth and happy work in 2022. Next time I come to Guangzhou, I will still choose to stay at the Oriental Hotel, a warm and charming place. Sorry, the review text is too much üòÑ
